  19 #include <dlfcn.h>
  20 #include <gconv.h>
  21 #include <stdint.h>
  22 
  23 /*
  24  * This module does conversions between gb2312 and big5 encodings.
  25  * It is necessary because gb2312 encoding use simplified chinese,
  26  * while big5 use traditional one. Often times both the simplified
  27  * version of a chinese character and its traditional counterpart
  28  * are presented in unicode and have distinctive code values. So
  29  * an indirect method through UCS4 (GB2312 <=> UCS4 <=> BIG5) will
  30  * not do the work correctly.
  31  *
  32  *   --- Yong Li  <rigel863@yahoo.com>
  33  */
  34 
  35

4775 
4776 /* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function.  */
4777 #define CHARSET_NAME        "EUC-CN//"
4778 #define FROM_LOOP       from_gb2312_to_big5
4779 #define TO_LOOP         from_big5_to_gb2312
4780 #define DEFINE_INIT     1
4781 #define DEFINE_FINI     1
4782 #define MIN_NEEDED_FROM     1
4783 #define MAX_NEEDED_FROM     2
4784 #define MIN_NEEDED_TO       1
4785 #define MAX_NEEDED_TO       2
4786 #define ONE_DIRECTION       0
4787 
4788 
4789 /* First define the conversion function from GB2312 to BIG5.  */
4790 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4791 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4792 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_TO
4793 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_TO
4794 #define LOOPFCT         FROM_LOOP
4795 #define BODY \
4796   {                                       \
4797     uint32_t ch = *inptr;                             \
4798                                           \
4799     if (ch <= 0x7f)                               \
4800       *outptr++ = *inptr++;                           \
4801     else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xf7)                        \
4802       {                                       \
4803     /* Two-byte character.  First test whether the                    \
4804        next byte is also available.  */                   \
4805     const char *cp;                               \
4806     int idx;                                  \
4807                                           \
4808     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
4809       {                                   \
4810         /* The second character is not available.  Store              \
4811            the intermediate result.  */                   \
4812         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
4813         break;                                \
4814       }                                   \
4815                                           \
4816     idx = (ch - 0xa1) * 94;                           \
4817     ch = inptr[1];                                    \
4818                                           \
4819     /* All second bytes of a multibyte character must be >= 0xa1. */      \
4820     if (__glibc_unlikely (ch < 0xa1))                     \
4821       {                                   \
4822         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4823         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
4824       }                                   \
4825                                           \
4826     idx += ch - 0xa1;                             \
4827                                           \
4828     /* Get the value from the table.  */                      \
4829     cp = __from_gb2312_to_big5[idx];                      \
4830     if (__glibc_unlikely (cp[0] == '\0'))                     \
4831       {                                   \
4832         /* We do not have a mapping for this character.           \
4833            If ignore errors, map it to 0xa1bc - big5 box character */     \
4834         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4835         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4836           break;                                  \
4837                                           \
4838         /* See if there is enough room to write the second byte. */       \
4839         if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend))              \
4840           {                                   \
4841         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4842             break;                                \
4843           }                                   \
4844                                           \
4845         *outptr++ = '\xa1';                           \
4846         *outptr++ = '\xbc';                           \
4847         inptr += 2;                               \
4848         ++*irreversible;                              \
4849         continue;                                 \
4850       }                                   \
4851     else                                      \
4852       {                                   \
4853         /* See whether there is enough room to write the second byte. */  \
4854         if (__builtin_expect (cp[1], '\1') != '\0'                \
4855             && __builtin_expect (outptr + 1 >= outend, 0))            \
4856           {                                   \
4857             /* We do not have enough room.  */                \
4858             result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4859             break;                                \
4860           }                                   \
4861                                           \
4862         *outptr++ = cp[0];                            \
4863         if (cp[1] != '\0')                            \
4864           *outptr++ = cp[1];                          \
4865       }                                   \
4866                                               \
4867     inptr += 2;                               \
4868       }                                       \
4869     else                                      \
4870       {                                       \
4871     /* This is illegal.  */                           \
4872     STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
4873       }                                       \
4874   }
4875 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4876 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4877 
4878 /* Next, define the other direction.  */
4879 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_TO
4880 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_TO
4881 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4882 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4883 #define LOOPFCT         TO_LOOP
4884 #define BODY \
4885   {                                       \
4886     uint32_t ch = *inptr;                             \
4887                                           \
4888     if (ch <= 0x7f)                               \
4889       *outptr++ = *inptr++;                           \
4890     else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xf9)                        \
4891       {                                       \
4892     /* Two byte character.  First test whether the                \
4893        next byte is also available.  */                   \
4894     const char *cp;                               \
4895     int idx;                                  \
4896                                           \
4897     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
4898       {                                   \
4899         /* The second character is not available.  Store              \
4900            the intermediate result.  */                   \
4901         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
4902         break;                                \
4903       }                                   \
4904                                           \
4905     idx = (ch - 0xa1) * 157;                          \
4906     ch = inptr[1];                                    \
4907     /* See if the second byte is in the correct range. */             \
4908     if (ch >= 0x40 && ch <= 0x7e)                         \
4909       idx += ch - 0x40;                           \
4910     else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xa1, 1)                 \
4911          && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xfe, 1))                 \
4912       idx += 0x3f + (ch - 0xa1);                          \
4913     else                                      \
4914       {                                   \
4915         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4916         STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
4917       }                                   \
4918                                           \
4919     /* Get the value from the table.  */                      \
4920     cp = __from_big5_to_gb2312 [idx];                     \
4921     if (__glibc_unlikely (cp[0] == '\0'))                     \
4922       {                                   \
4923         /* We do not have a mapping for this character.           \
4924            If ignore errors, map it to 0xa1f5 - gb box character */       \
4925         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4926         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4927           break;                                  \
4928                                           \
4929         /* See if there is enough room to write the second byte. */       \
4930         if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend))              \
4931           {                                   \
4932         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4933             break;                                \
4934           }                                   \
4935                                           \
4936         *outptr++ = '\xa1';                           \
4937         *outptr++ = '\xf5';                           \
4938         inptr += 2;                               \
4939         ++*irreversible;                              \
4940         continue;                                 \
4941       }                                   \
4942     else                                      \
4943       {                                   \
4944         /* see if there is enough room to write the second byte. */       \
4945         if (__builtin_expect (cp[1], '\1') != '\0'                \
4946             && __builtin_expect (outptr + 1 >= outend, 0))            \
4947           {                                   \
4948             /* We do not have enough room.  */                \
4949             result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4950             break;                                \
4951           }                                   \
4952                                           \
4953         *outptr++ = cp[0];                            \
4954         if (cp[1] != '\0')                            \
4955           *outptr++ = cp[1];                          \
4956       }                                   \
4957                                               \
4958     inptr += 2;                               \
4959       }                                       \
4960     else                                      \
4961       {                                       \
4962     /* This is illegal.  */                           \
4963     STANDARD_FROM_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (1);                   \
4964       }                                       \
4965   }
4966 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4967 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4968 
4969 /* Now define the toplevel functions.  */
4970 #include <iconv/skeleton.c>
